# Text Elements
Pressure - Volume ^eyDKzznr

Pressure - Temperature ^ersLEKKW

Volume - Temperature ^7ueVMqpZ

Increase in Temperature cause
the particles to gain more K.E
they get faster
they hit the container more frequently
with more force

Pressure increases ^ZAnut4dd

Expandable ^hvhvYkyo

Not expandable ^qolDh3uV

Increase in Temperature causes
the particles to gain more K.E
they get faster
and (try) to consume more space
hence

Volume increases ^sSVsx29b

Pressure is caused by the particles
colliding with the surface of the container

The particles COLLIDE WITH THE SURFACE
more FREQUENTLY when volume decreases
and with more force (higher pressure)

Hence Pressure increases ^Ni5bhEt0

%%
